# Get Separatist Faction for Planets, Generic
get_planet_separatist_faction_gen = {
		 if = { limit = { NOT = { exists = event_target:p_separatist_1 } } save_global_event_target_as = p_separatist_1 set_planet_flag = p_separatist_1 }

# Defeated/Extinct Nations
get_planet_separatist_faction_nat = {
		 if = { limit = { NOT = { exists = event_target:p_nat_separatist_1 } } save_global_event_target_as = p_nat_separatist_1 set_planet_flag = p_nat_separatist_1 }
	else_if = { limit = { NOT = { exists = event_target:p_nat_separatist_2 } } save_global_event_target_as = p_nat_separatist_2 set_planet_flag = p_nat_separatist_2 }
	else_if = { limit = { NOT = { exists = event_target:p_nat_separatist_3 } } save_global_event_target_as = p_nat_separatist_3 set_planet_flag = p_nat_separatist_3 }
	else_if = { limit = { NOT = { exists = event_target:p_nat_separatist_4 } } save_global_event_target_as = p_nat_separatist_4 set_planet_flag = p_nat_separatist_4 }
	else_if = { limit = { NOT = { exists = event_target:p_nat_separatist_5 } } save_global_event_target_as = p_nat_separatist_5 set_planet_flag = p_nat_separatist_5 }
	else_if = { limit = { NOT = { exists = event_target:p_nat_separatist_6 } } save_global_event_target_as = p_nat_separatist_6 set_planet_flag = p_nat_separatist_6 }
	else_if = { limit = { NOT = { exists = event_target:p_nat_separatist_7 } } save_global_event_target_as = p_nat_separatist_7 set_planet_flag = p_nat_separatist_7 }
	else_if = { limit = { NOT = { exists = event_target:p_nat_separatist_8 } } save_global_event_target_as = p_nat_separatist_8 set_planet_flag = p_nat_separatist_8 }
	else_if = { limit = { NOT = { exists = event_target:p_nat_separatist_9 } } save_global_event_target_as = p_nat_separatist_9 set_planet_flag = p_nat_separatist_9 }

	else_if = { limit = { NOT = { exists = event_target:p_nat_separatist_11 } } save_global_event_target_as = p_nat_separatist_11 set_planet_flag = p_nat_separatist_11 }
